   4              	{       Copyright(c): Leon de Boer(LdB) 2017								}

   8              	{																            }
   9              	{     This sourcecode is released for the purpose to promote programming    }
  10              	{  on the Raspberry Pi. You may redistribute it and/or modify with the      }
  11              	{  following disclaimer and condition.                                      }
  12              	{																            }
  13              	{      The SOURCE CODE is distributed "AS IS" WITHOUT WARRANTIES AS TO      }
  14              	{   PERFORMANCE OF MERCHANTABILITY WHETHER EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED.            }
  15              	{   Redistributions of source code must retain the copyright notices to     }
  16              	{   maintain the author credit (attribution) .								}
  17              	{																			}
  18              	{***************************************************************************}
  19              	{                                                                           }
  20              	{       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for   }
  21              	{  the Pi 1/2/3. It simplifies some of the autodetect code but importantly  }
  22              	{  directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that it provides   }
  23              	{  stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader spinlock     }
  24              	{  that protects against registers R0-R3 trashed. As any C/C++ compiler     }
  25              	{  code will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore programming   }
  26              	{  this protection must be done.											}
  27              	{       The downside is this bootstub must be a little more complex in      }
  28              	{  that it must start and setup multiple cores. The code is much more       }
  29              	{  connected to the linker file which provides memory space to each core.   }
  30              	{        There is however matching paired AARCH64 stub and linker files     }
  31              	{  so code written for this setup can be ported to AARCH64 with ease.		}
  32              	{																            }
  33              	{++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++*/
  34              	
  35              	/*==========================================================================}
  36              	;{				 	 ARM CPU ID CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    }
  37              	;{=========================================================================*/
  38              	#define ARM6_CPU_ID 0x410FB767					// CPU id a BCM2835 reports
  39              	#define ARM7_CPU_ID 0x410FC073					// CPU id a BCM2836 reports
  40              	#define ARM8_CPU_ID 0x410FD034					// CPU id a BCM2837 reports
  41              	
  42              	/*==========================================================================}
  43              	;{				 	 ARM CPU MODE CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    }
  44              	;{=========================================================================*/
  45              	#define CPU_FIQMODE 0x11						// CPU in FIQ mode
  46              	#define CPU_IRQMODE 0x12						// CPU in IRQ mode
  47              	#define CPU_SVCMODE 0x13						// CPU in SVC mode
  48              	#define CPU_HYPMODE 0x1A						// CPU in HYP mode
  49              	
  50              	/*==========================================================================}
  51              	;{				 ARM CPU IRQ/FIQ BIT CONSTANT DEFINITIONS				    }
  52              	;{=========================================================================*/
  53              	#define I_Bit  (1 << 7)							// Irq flag bit in cpsr (CPUMODE register)
  54              	#define F_Bit  (1 << 6)							// Fiq flag bit in cpsr (CPUMODE register)
ARM GAS  C:\Users\ldebo\AppData\Local\Temp\cc0w9t1b.s 			page 2

  76              	.arm
  77              	_start:
  78              	;@"================================================================"
  79              	;@ Grab cpu mode and start address and hold in a high register.
  80              	;@"================================================================"
  81 0000 0FC0A0E1 		mov r12, pc;							;@ Hold boot address in high register R12
  82 0004 00B00FE1 		mrs r11, CPSR							;@ Read current CPU mode
  83 0008 1FB00BE2 		and r11, r11, #0x1F						;@ Clear all but CPU mode bits in register r11
  84              	;@"================================================================"
  85              	;@ If the cpu is in HYP_MODE(EL2) we will bring it SVC_MODE (EL1).
  86              	;@"================================================================"
  87              	multicore_start:
  88 000c 00000FE1 	    mrs r0,cpsr								;@ Fetch the cpsr register which includes CPU mode bits 
  89 0010 1F1000E2 	 	and r1, r0, #0x1F						;@ Mask off the CPU mode bits to register r1                            
  90 0014 1A0051E3 	 	cmp r1, #CPU_HYPMODE					;@ Check we are in HYP_MODE											
  91 0018 0500001A 		bne .NotInHypMode						;@ Branch if not equal meaning was not in HYP_MODE  
  92 001c 1F00C0E3 		bic r0,r0,#0x1F							;@ Clear the CPU mode bits in register r0							
  93 0020 D30080E3 		orr r0, r0, #CPU_SVCMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit;@ Logical OR SVC_MODE bits onto register with Irq/Fiq dis
  94 0024 00F06FE1 	    msr spsr_cxsf,r0						;@ Hold value in spsr_cxsf
  95 0028 04E08FE2 	    add lr,pc,#4							;@ Calculate address of .NotInHypMode label
  96              		/* I borrowed this trick from Ultibo because ARM6 code running on an ARM7/8 needs this opcode  */
  97              		/* The ARM6 compiler does not know these instructions so it is a way to get needed opcode here */
  98              	    /* So our ARM6 code can drop an arm7 or arm8 out of HYP mode and run on an ARM7/8.             
  99              	 	/* Native ARM7/8 compilers already understand the OPCODE but do not mind it this way either	   */
 100 002c 0EF32EE1 		.long 0xE12EF30E						;@ "msr ELR_hyp, lr" Set the address to ELR_hyp
 101 0030 6E0060E1 		.long 0xE160006E						;@ "eret" Elevated return which will exit at .NotInHypMode in SVC_MODE
 102              	.NotInHypMode:
 103              	;@"================================================================"
 104              	;@  Setup stack pointers for each core and each CPU operation mode
 105              	;@"================================================================"
 106 0034 4C229FE5 	    ldr r2, = __SVC_stack_core0				;@ Address of svc_stack_core0 stack pointer value
 107 0038 4C329FE5 	    ldr r3, = __FIQ_stack_core0				;@ Address of fiq_stack_core0 stack pointer value
 108 003c 4C429FE5 	    ldr r4, = __IRQ_stack_core0				;@ Address of irq_stack_core0 stack pointer value
 109 0040 100F10EE 		mrc p15, 0, r0, c0, c0, 0				;@ Read CPU ID Register
